 Daniel Mukhi of Indian origin became the first leader in Australia to take oath in New South Wales Parliament on Tuesday
 mukhi (32) ko lebar party ne new south wales ke upari sadan main steve whon ke sthaan par chunaa gaya he
 Mukhi is the first leader of Indian background in the province
 unhone kaha, yah bahut sammaan kii baat he or mujhe is baat kii khushi he ki main gita par haath rakhkar nishtha kii shapath lene vaala pehla austrailian rajaneta ban gaya hum
 Mukhi said that Gita is one of the great religious texts of the world like the Bible and Quran
 unhone kaha ki vah is mukaam par isliye pahunche hai, kyonki austrailia mere mata pita jaise logon ke yogadan kaa swaagat karata he
 He hoped that he would put his voice firmly in the Upper House of NSW and work for the good of the people
 mukhi ke mata pita 1973 main punjab se australia aae the
 Born in Blacktown, Mukhi has three university degrees and is currently working as an advisor to organizations, charities and community groups

 is circular main hi yah protocol tha

 Many states of the country are struggling with cash crisis
 iske peeche bhale hi kai kaaran bataae ja rahe hon, lekin desh kii note press kii ise lekar kuch or hi kahani he
 According to sources, the Rs 500 note has not been printed in Nashik's note press since last November
 jabaki press main april se 200, 100 or 50 rupee ke noton kii printing main 44 pratishat kii kami hui he
 According to media reports, the press stopped the printing of notes due to the completion of 2017-18 target
 nasik printing press ko arabiai ne 18 million note chhapane kaa target diya tha
 Similarly, printing of 20 and 100 rupee notes was also stopped on 1 April
 iske peeche kaaran nae noton kii dizine kaa bataaya ja rahaa he
 As far as the 200 rupee note is concerned, the RBI ordered the printing of its 200 note in Madhya Pradesh, Note Press Dewas, after which the printing of 200 note was stopped in Nashik
 philhalanasik note presskeval 10 or 50 rupee ke noton kii chapai kar rahaa he
 Sources say that the printing of notes has fallen from 18 million to 10 million pieces
 jiske baad april 16 se nasik note press ne dobaaraa 500 noton kii printing shuru kii he
